function Alert( swal_params, swal_params2, swal_params3 ) {
  swal.setDefaults({ showCancelButton: false });
  if( swal_params2 )
  {
    swal({ title: swal_params, text: swal_params2, type: swal_params3 });

function Confirm( swal_params, callback_true ) {
  swal.setDefaults({ showCancelButton: true });
  if( callback_true ) {
    swal({ title: "", text: swal_params }, function(isConfirm) { callback_true(isConfirm); });
  }
  else
  {
    swal( swal_params );
  }

      functionReady: function( origin, content ) {

        { 
          jQuery(origin).tooltipster('option', 'position', 'top' ); 
          var el_left = -1 * ( jQuery(origin).width() / 2 );

            el_left = el_left + parseInt(jQuery(origin).attr("tooltipster_left")); 
          }
          jQuery(origin).tooltipster('option', 'offsetX', el_left );

        else

        if( jQuery(origin).hasClass("tooltipster-focus") )  {

        jQuery(origin).tooltipster('reposition');

// Hide Header on on scroll down
var didScroll;
var lastScrollTop = 0;
var delta = 5;
var navbarHeight = jQuery('div#header').outerHeight();

jQuery(window).scroll(function(event){
    didScroll = true;
});

setInterval(function() {
    if (didScroll) {
        hasScrolled();
        didScroll = false;
    }
}, 250);

function hasScrolled() {
  var st = jQuery(this).scrollTop();

  if(Math.abs(lastScrollTop - st) <= delta)
  {
    return;
  }  

  var up = 0;
  if( st < 165 )
  {
    jQuery('div#header').removeClass('header-up').removeClass('header-down').removeClass('header-hidden');
    up = 1;
    jQuery('div#content,body').removeClass('pushed');
  }
  else if( st > 210 )
  {
    jQuery('div#header').addClass('header-hidden').removeClass('header-up').removeClass('header-down');
    up=0;
  }

  if (st > lastScrollTop && st > navbarHeight)
  {} else
  {
    if( st + jQuery(window).height() < jQuery(document).height() && up == 0) 
    {
      jQuery('div#header').addClass('header-up').removeClass('header-hidden').removeClass('header-down');
      jQuery('div#content,body').addClass('pushed');
    }
    else
    {
      jQuery('div#content,body').removeClass('pushed');
    }
  }
  lastScrollTop = st;
}

    jQuery("ul#mobinavi").find("a.selected:last").parent().parent().find(".mobinav-toggler").addClass("mobinav-toggler-minus");
    jQuery("ul#mobinavi").find("a.selected:last").css("font-weight","bold");
    jQuery("ul#mobinavi").find("a.selected:last").parent().parent().parent().next("ul").show();
    jQuery("ul#mobinavi").hide();                                                       
  }

});
//-->
      </script>

function hideResults() {
  var i=0;
  jQuery("ul.ui-menu li").hide();
  jQuery("ul.ui-menu li").each( function() {
    if(i <= 20)
    {
      jQuery(this).show();
    }
    i++;
  });
}

var source = null;
var lastXhr = null;
var queryTerm = "";
var lastTerm = "";
var cacheData = [];

jQuery("document").ready( function() {
  jQuery("span#fld-min-len").html("3");
  jQuery("#search").live("focus", function(e) {

    jQuery(".ac-search-help").hide();
    jQuery("#autocomplete-no-results").hide();  

    if( 1==1 )
    {
      if( jQuery(this).val() == "" || jQuery(this).val() == jQuery(this).attr("title") || jQuery(this).val().length < 3 )
      {
        jQuery("#ac-search-help").show();
      }
    }

    if( jQuery(this).val().length >= 3 )
    {
        jQuery("#autocomplete-results").show();
    }
  });

  jQuery("#search").live("blur", function() {
    jQuery("#autocomplete-no-results").hide();  
//    setTimeout(function() { jQuery("#autocomplete-results").hide(); }, 1000);
    jQuery("#ac-search-help").hide();
  });

  jQuery("#search").live("keyup", function() {
    jQuery("#autocomplete-no-results").hide();  
    var len = jQuery(this).val().length;
    if(len < 3)
    {
      jQuery("#autocomplete-results .ui-menu").hide();
      jQuery(".ac-search-help").hide();
      jQuery("#ac-search-help").show();
    }
  });

  jQuery("select[name=ryhma_id]").live("change click",function() {
    jQuery("#autocomplete-no-results").hide();  
    if( jQuery("#search").val() && jQuery("#search").val() != 'Hakusana(t)' )
    {
      queryTerm = "";
      jQuery("#search").autocomplete("search");
    }
  });

  jQuery("form#contact-search-form").submit(function() {
    if( (!jQuery("#search").val() || jQuery("#search").val() == 'Hakusana(t)') && 0 == 1)
    {
      jQuery("#search").val("*").css("color","transparent");
    }
  });



jQuery("#search").autocomplete({
  appendTo: "#autocomplete-results",
  minLength: 3,
  position: {  collision: "flip horizontal"  },
  select: function(event, ui) {
            jQuery("#ac-search-help").hide();
	    if (ui.item.url) {
	        if( ui.item.target ) {
                  window.open( ui.item.url, ui.item.target);
                  setTimeout(function() { jQuery("#search").val("").blur();}, 100);
                }
                else {
                  window.location.href=ui.item.url;
                }
	    }
	    else {
                var use_utf8 = "1";
                var label = ui.item.label;
                if( use_utf8 )
                {
                  label = encodeURIComponent(label);
                }
		window.location.href = "/jarvenpaa/haku.tmpl?search=1;full_and_free=1;sivu_id=3;free_text_value=" + label;
	    }
  },
  source: function(request, response) {

	    //
	    // Jos term alusta mätsää aiemmin haussa käytettyyn queryTermiin
	    // ja queryTerm ei ole tyhjä, käytetään cachettua hakutulosta.
	    // Muussa tapauksessa tehdään uusi haku
	    // 
	    
	    var term = request.term.toLowerCase();
	    lastTerm = term;

	    if( 1==0 )
            {
              queryTerm = "";
            }

	    if (queryTerm != "" && term.match(queryTerm)) {
		var data = [];
                if(data.length == 0)
                {
                  jQuery("#autocomplete-no-results").show();
                }
		for (var i=0; i<cacheData.length; i++) {
		    if (cacheData[i].label.toLowerCase().match(term)) {
			data.push(cacheData[i]);
                        jQuery("#autocomplete-no-results").hide();
		    }
                    else
                    {
                      if(data.length == 0)
                      {
                        jQuery("#autocomplete-no-results").show();
                      }
                      jQuery('.ui-autocomplete-loading').removeClass("ui-autocomplete-loading");
                    }
		}
                jQuery("#ac-search-help").hide();
		response(data);
                hideResults();
 		return;
	    }

	    request.term = term; // lowerace
	    queryTerm = term;
            request.limit = 999999; //20;
            request.show_ancestors = 1;
            request.min_length = 3;
            request.lang = 'fi';
            

	    lastXhr = $.getJSON( "/jarvenpaa/ac_list.tmpl", request, function( data, status, xhr ) {

                    if( data.length == "0")
                    {
                      jQuery("#autocomplete-no-results").show();
                      jQuery("#autocomplete-results").hide();
                    }
                    else
                    {
                      jQuery("#autocomplete-results").show();
                      jQuery("#autocomplete-no-results").hide();
                    }
                    jQuery("#ac-search-help").hide();
   
		    cacheData = data;
		    if ( xhr === lastXhr ) {
			response( data );
		    }

                    jQuery('.ui-autocomplete-loading').removeClass("ui-autocomplete-loading");

                    hideResults();

		});
	}
	
  })
  .data( "autocomplete" )._renderItem = function( ul, item ) {

    // korostetaan hakutermiä vastaava osuus boldaamalla
    // Toimii nyt myös keskeltä, esim linkkitekstin toinen sana.

//    var label = '<b>' +
//    item.label.substring(0, lastTerm.length) + '</b>' + 
//    item.label.substring(lastTerm.length);

      var re = new RegExp('(' + lastTerm + ')', 'gi');
      var label= item.label;
      label = label.replace(re, '<b>$1</b>');

    //var re = new RegExp('^'.lastTerm, "i");
    if (item.url) {
	return $( '<li></li>' )
	.data( "item.autocomplete", item )
	.append( "<a><nobr><img src='/common_ui/embed_ui/img/icons_google/extra/ic_page_black_18dp.png' alt='' class='absmiddle'> /" + item.path + label + "</nobr></a>" )
	.appendTo( ul );
    }
    else {
	return $( "<li></li>" )
	.data( "item.autocomplete", item )
	.append( "<a>" + label + "</a>" )
	.appendTo( ul );
    }


  };
});
